 Sehwag finally took the wickets of Brett Lee (4) and then Daniel Christian (24)
 2008 main ‘mankigate’ ghatana kaa gavaah rahaa sidney cricket ground (esasiji) maidan par bharatiyon dwaara 24wein over main david hassi ke khilaaf ‘obstruction of da field’ kii apil charchaa kaa vishay rahi, jise maidani ampiron ne tisare ampire simon frai ke nirdesh par khaarij kar diya or faisla ballebaaj ke paksh main rahaa
 The run-out of Sachin Tendulkar (14) during the seventh over of the Indian innings also became quite tense
 brett lee ke over kii antim gend par gambhir ne tendulkar ko ek ran ke liye bulaayaa or vah ran ke liye daud pade
 But while completing the run, Lee stood in the way of Tendulkar and was dismissed by David Warner
 tendulkar ne hataasha main apane haath hawa main uthaae, lekin squaire leg par khadey ampire simon tuffel or billy boden ne charchaa ke baad ballebaaj ke khilaaf faisla sunaaya
 Earlier, after winning the toss, the Australian team battled losing three wickets for 57 runs in the 14th over but managed to score from the half-centuries of David Warner (68), David Hussey (54) and Matthew Wade (56)
 vinay kumaar kii mansapeshiyon main khinchaav kii chot ke kaaran antim ekadash main shaamil praveen kumaar ne shuru main do wicket chatkaakar acchhee shuruyaat dilaai
 Umesh Yadav took two wickets in the final two overs, but Sehwag proved to be the surprise package, taking three wickets for 43 runs in his nine overs
 antim 10 over main bharat ne keval 47 ran hi kharch kiye
 Praveen bowled Maiden over first and then Watson (1) and Peter Forrest (7) cheaply paved the way for the pavilion
 unhone saat over main 22 ran dekar do wicket praapt kiye
 Watson bridges Praveen's short pitch ball, which goes into the hands of fielder Umesh Yadav at mid-on, while Forrest attempts to cut the bouncing ball, which is close to him, and it straight up his stumps
 
 warner or mike hassi (10) ne shuruaati jhatkon kii bharpai karne kii koshish kii, lekin mike hassi doosraa ran lene kii gafalat main ran out ho gaye
 He sent r Ashwin to the long off and with the consent of his partner Warner, ran in an attempt to take a second run
 lekin warner ne iraadaa badal diya or hassi waapas naan striker krij par lautne kii sthiti main nahin the
 Fielder Pathan threw a good throw and Ashwin did not delay at all
 is samay 14wein over tak australia ne 57 ran par teen wicket ganvaa die the
 India hooked up medium-pacer Yadav in the 15th over and the team lost its grip here
 yadav ne apane do over main 20 ran ganvaae or isi dauraan warner ne unki gend par chaukaa lagaakar apana ardhashatak puraa kiya, jiske liye unhone 48 gend kaa saamana kiya or paanch chauke lagaae
 As soon as the Australian team completed 100 innings, Warner caught Suresh Raina in the 21st over to sweep Ravindra Jadeja's ball
 raina or pathan donon is kaich ko lapakane kii koshish main jor se takaraa bhi gaye, haalanki unhen koi gambhir chot nahin lagi
 Warner added 68 runs in his innings with the help of seven fours in 66 balls, Australia were in trouble after losing four wickets for 107 runs
 iske baad 'obstruction of da field' kii apil austrailia ke paksh main gai
 The comments vade or david hassi ne iske baad behtareen stroke lagaakar team ko is kathin sthiti se baahar nikaala
 At the same time, Wade completed a half-century by hitting a high six over midwicket off Ashwin
 haalanki baayen haath ke ballebaaj vade 40wein over main yadav kii gend par wicket ke peeche dhoni ko aasaan kaich dekar out ho gaye
 He scored 56 runs in 66 balls with two fours and a six
 unhone david hassi ke saath paanchaven wicket ke liye 110 gend main 94 ran kii bhagidaari kii
 In the same over, David Hussey completed his 50 runs in 58 balls with the help of two fours and the Australian team scored 205 for five by the end of this over
 yadav ne junior hassi kaa wicket hasil kiya, jo unki gend par dhoni ko kaich dekar out hue

 Praveen Kumar, who was included in the playing XI due to a hamstring injury to Vinay Kumar, got off to a good start with two wickets in the beginning
 umesh yadav ne antim do over main do wicket hasil kiye, lekin sahvaag ascharyajanak package sabit hue, jinhone apane nau over main 43 ran dekar teen wicket hasil kiye
 India spent only 47 runs in the last 10 overs
 praveen ne pehla over madan phenkaa or phir watasan (1) or peter forest (7) ko saste main pavilion kii raah dikhaai
 He took two wickets for 22 runs in seven overs
 watasan ne praveen kii short pich gend ko pul kiya, jo mid on main khadey kshetrarakshak umesh yadav ke haathon main chali gai, jabaki forest ne uchhalati hui gend ko cat karne kaa prayaas kiya, jo unke kaaphi kareeb thi or yah sidhe unke stump ukhaad gai
 Warner and Mike Hussey (10) tried to make up for the early setbacks, but Mike Hussey was run out trying to take a second run
 unhone aar aswin kii gend ko long of kii taraf bheja or apane jodidar warner kii sahmati se doosraa ran lene ke prayaas main daud pade
 But Warner changed his mind and Hussey was not in a position to return to the non-striker crease
 kshetrarakshak pathan ne acha thro phenkaa or aswin ne unhen out karne main jaraa bhi deree nahin kii
 By this time Australia had lost three wickets for 57 runs by the 14th over
 bharat ne 15wein over main madhyam gati ke gendbaaj yadav ko lagaaya or yaheen team kii pakad dhili ho gai
 Yadav missed 20 runs in his two overs and in the meantime Warner completed his half-century with a four off his ball, for which he faced 48 balls and hit five fours
 jaise hi australian team ne pari ke 100 ran puure kiye, warner 21wein over main rabindra jadeja kii gend ko sweep karne ke chakkar main suresh raina ko kaich de baithe
 Raina and Pathan both hit hard in an attempt to catch the catch, although they did not get any serious injuries
 warner ne apni pari main 66 gend main saat chauke kii madad se 68 ran jode, unke out hone par australia 107 ran par chaar wicket ganvaakar mushkil main tha
 After this, the appeal of 'obstruction of the Field' went in favor of Australia
 tippaniyan Wade and David Hussey then put the team out of this difficult situation with excellent strokes
 isi dauraan vade ne aswin kii gend par midwicket par gaganchumbi chakka lagaakar ardhashatak puraa kiya
 However, left-handed batsman Wade was dismissed in the 40th over with a simple catch to Dhoni behind the wicket off Yadav

 ' Priyanka Chopra and Farhan Akhtar starrer film The Sky is Pink has been released in all theaters from today
 is film ko lekar sabhi ke bich kaaphi utsaah tha or phens iskaa besabri se intjaar kar rahe the
 Now that the film has been released, the fans are expressing their love for it
 priyanka chopra, farhaan akhtar or rohit saraaf kaaphi samay se filmad ski ij pinkka jamkar pramotion kar rahe hai
 Not only this, Priyanka is now promoting her film by going to big talk shows in America
 iske liye priyanka kii khub tarif bhi ho rahi he
 After watching Priyanka and Farhan's film, everyone from celebrities to fans became emotional
 aaysha choudhary naam kii ladki or uske parivaar kii ye kahani behad khubasurat or imotional or phens bataa rahe hai ki kaise wo film ko dekhakar khub roe
 Not only this, the work of Zaira Wasim, Farhan Akhtar, Rohit Saraf and other supporting actors is also being praised in the film with Priyanka Chopra
